vedanākkhandho saññākkhandho saṅkhārakkhandho viññāṇakkhandho Rūpaṃ rūpakkhandho rūpakkhandho rūpaṃ vedanā vedanākkhandho vedanākkhandho vedanā saññā saññākkhandho saññākkhandho saññā saṅkhārā saṅkhārakkhandho saṅkhārakkhandho saṅkhārā viññāṇaṃ viññāṇakkhandho viññāṇakkhandho viññāṇaṃ Na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho na rūpakkhandho na rūpaṃ na vedanā    pe    na saññā    pe    na saṅkhārā    pe    na viññāṇaṃ na viññāṇakkhandhona viññāṇakkhandho na viññāṇaṃ Rūpaṃ rūpakkhandho khandhā vedanākkhandhorūpaṃ rūpakkhandho khandhā saññākkhandho rūpaṃ rūpakkhandho khandhā saṅkhārakkhandho rūpaṃ rūpakkhandho khandhā viññāṇakkhandho Vedanā vedanākkhandho khandhā rūpakkhandho    khandhā viññāṇakkhandho Saññā saññākkhandho khandhā rūpakkhandho   khandhā viññāṇakkhandho Saṅkhārā saṅkhārakkhandho khandhā rūpakkhandho    khandhā viññāṇakkhandho Viññāṇaṃ viññāṇakkhandho khandhā rūpakkhandho    khandhā saṅkhārakkhandho Na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho na khandhā na vedanākkhandho na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho na khandhā na saññākkhandhoKhandhayamakaṃ               na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho na khandhā na saṅkhārakkhandho na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho na khandhā na viññāṇakkhandho Na vedanā na vedanākkhandho    na viññāṇakkhandho    Na saññā na saññākkhandho    na viññāṇakkhandho Na saṅkhārā na saṅkhārakkhandho    na viññāṇakkhandhoNa viññāṇaṃ na viññāṇakkhandho    na saṅkhārakkhandho Rūpaṃ khandho khandhā rūpaṃ vedanā khandhokhandhā vedanā saññā khandho khandhā saññā saṅkhārā khandho khandhā saṅkhārā viññāṇaṃ khandhokhandhā viññāṇaṃ Na rūpaṃ na khandho na khandhā na rūpaṃ na vedanā    na viññāṇaṃ na khandho na khandhā na viññānaṃ Rūpaṃ khandho khandhā vedanā rūpaṃ khandhokhandhā saññā    saṅkhārā    khandhā viññāṇaṃ Vedanā khandho khandhā rūpaṃ vedanā khandho khandhā saññā    khandhā viññānaṃ khandho                             Khandhayamakaṃkhandhā rūpaṃ viññāṇaṃ khandho khandhā vedanā    khandhā saṅkhārā Na rūpaṃ na khandho na khandhā na vedanā na rūpaṃ na khandho na khandhā na saññā vedanākkhandho ti Vedanākkh khandho ceva vedanākkh ca avasesā khandhā khandhā na vedanākkhandho   a and b are each repeated three times each of the remaining khandhas being substituted in turn in b for vedanāc Vedanā vedanākkhandho ti Āmantā b Khandhā rūpakkhandho ti Rūpakkhandho khandho ceva rūpakkhca avasesā khandhā khandhā na rūpakkh   c and b are each repeated as in the case of a and b So also for d Saññā saññākkhandho ti Diṭṭhisaññā saññāna saññākkh saññākkh saññā ceva saññākkh ca for e Saṅkhārā saṅkhārakkhandho ti Saṅkhārakkhandhaṃ ṭhapetvā avasesā saṅkhārā saṅkhārā na saṅkhārakkhsaṅkhārakkh saṅkhārā ceva saṅkhārakkh ca and for f Viññāṇaṃ viññāṇakkhandho ti Āmantā  sets of questions and  answers each                        Khandhayamakaṃ a Na rūpaṃ na rūpakkhandho ti Āmantā b Na khandhā na vedanākkhandho ti Āmantā   Here again a is made to alternate times with b the other khandhas being substituted in b in sucession with the invarible reply Āmantā Then Na vedanā etc replaces Na rūpaṃ etc and b commences with Na khandhā na rūpakkhandho ti So on for the other three khandhas Rūpaṃ khandho ti Āmantā Khandhā rūpakkhandho ti Rūpakkh khandho ceva rūpakkh dhammāy ca uppajjati manāy ca uppajjatiiii Yassa yattha cakkhāy uppajjati tassa tattha sotāyuppajjatīti Sacakkhukānaṃ asotakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha cakkhāy uppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha sotāyuppajjati sacakkhukānaṃ sasotakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha cakkhāy ca uppajjati sotāy ca uppajjatiYassa vā pana yattha sotāy uppajjati tassa tattha cakkhāy uppajjatīti Sasotakānaṃ acakkhukānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha sotāy uppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha cakkhāy uppajjati sasotakānaṃ sacakkhukānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha sotāy ca uppajjati cakkhāy ca uppajjati Saṅkhittaṃ yass ekasadisaṃYassa yattha manāy uppajjati tassa tattha dhammāyuppajjatīti Āmantā Yassa vā pana yattha dhammāyuppajjati tassa tattha manāy uppajjatīti Acittakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha dhammāy uppajjatīti Kāmāvacarā cavantānaṃ aghānakānaṃ kāmāvacaraṃ uppajjantānaṃ rūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha rūpāy                       Āyatanayamakaṃuppajjittha no ca tesaṃ tattha ghānāy uppajjati saghānakānaṃ kāmāvacaraṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha rūpāy ca uppajjittha ghānāyca uppajjatiYassa yattha ghānāy uppajjati tassa tattha manāyuppajjitthāti Āmantā Yassa vā pana yattha manāyuppajjittha tassa tattha ghānāy uppajjatīti Kāmāvacarā cavantānaṃ aghānakānaṃ kāmāvacaraṃ uppajjantānaṃ rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesan tattha manāy uppajjittha no ca tesan tattha ghānāy uppajjati saghānakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manāy ca uppajjittha ghānāyca uppajjatiYassa yattha ghānāy uppajjati tassa tattha dhammāyuppajjitthāti Āmantā Yassa vā pana yattha dhammāyuppajjittha tassa tattha ghānāy uppajjatīti Sabbesaṃ cavantānaṃ aghānakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha dhammāy uppajjittha no ca tesan tattha ghānāyuppajjati saghānakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha dhammāy ca uppajjittha ghānāy ca uppajjatiYassa yattha rūpāy uppajjati tassa tattha manāyuppajjitthāti Suddhāvāsaṃ uppajjantānaṃ asaññasattaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha rūpāy uppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha manāy uppajjittha itaresaṃ pañcavokāraṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesan tattha rūpāy ca uppajjati manāy ca uppajjittha Yassa vā pana yattha manāy uppajjitthatassa tattha rūpāy uppajjatīti Pañcavokārā cavantānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manāy uppajjittha no ca tesaṃ tattha rūpāy uppajjati pañcavokāraṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manāy ca uppajjittha rūpāy ca uppajjatiĀyatanayamakaṃ                     Yassa yattha rūpāy uppajjati tassa tattha dhammāyuppajjitthāti Suddhāvāsaṃ uppajjantānan tesaṃ tattha rūpāy uppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha dhammāy uppajjitthaitaresaṃ sarūpakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha rūpāyca uppajjati dhammāy ca uppajjittha Yassa vā pana yattha dhammāy uppajjittha tassa tattha rūpāy uppajjatīti Sabbesaṃ cavantānaṃ arūpakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha dhammāy uppajjittha no ca tesaṃ tattha rūpāy uppajjati sarūpakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha dhammāy ca uppajjittha rūpāy ca uppajjatiYassa yattha manāy uppajjati tassa tattha dhammāyuppajjitthāti Suddhāvāsaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manāy uppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha dhammāy uppajjittha itaresaṃ sacittakānaṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manāy ca uppajjati dhammāy ca uppajjittha Yassa vā pana yattha dhammāy uppajjittha tassa tattha manāyuppajjatīti nuppajjitthāti UppajjitthaYassa vā pana dhammāy nuppajjittha tassa cakkhāynuppajjatīti Natthi etcYassa ghānāy    pe    rūpāy manāy nuppajjatitassa dhammāy nuppajjitthāti Uppajjittha Yassa vā pana dhammāy                       Āyatanayamakaṃnuppajjittha tassa manāy nuppajjatītiNatthi etcii Yattha cakkhāy nuppajjati    pe   iii Yassa yattha cakkhāy nuppajjati tassa tattha sotāy nuppajjitthāti Pañcavokārā cavantānaṃ acakkhukānaṃ kāmāvacaraṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha cakkhāynuppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha sotāy nuppajjittha suddhāvāse parinibbantānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha cakkhāy ca nuppajjati sotāy ca nuppajjitthaYassa vā pana yattha sotāy nuppajjittha tassa tattha cakkhāy nuppajjatīti Suddhāvāsan uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha sotāy nuppajjittha no ca tesaṃ tattha cakkhāynuppajjati suddhāvāse parinibbantānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha sotāy ca nuppajjittha cakkhāy ca nuppajjatiYassa yattha cakkhāy nuppajjati tassa tattha ghānāynuppajjitthāti nuppajjati ghānāy ca nuppajjittha Yassa vā pana yattha ghānāy nuppajjittha tassa tattha cakkhāy nuppajjitīti Rūpāvacaraṃ uppajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānāynuppajjittha no ca tesaṃ tattha cakkhāy tassa dhammāy nirujjhatītiĀmantā Yassa vā pana dhammāy nirujjhati tassa rūpāynirujjhatīti Arūpakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ dhammāynirujjhati no ca tesaṃ rūpāy nirujjhati sarūpakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ dhammāy ca nirujjhati rūpāy ca nirujjhatiYassa manāy nirujjhati tassa dhammāy nirujjhatītiĀmantā Yassa vā pana dhammāy nirujjhati tassa manāy nirujjhatīti Acittakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ dhammāy sadisaṃ etciii Yassa yattha cakkhāy nirujjhati tassa tattha sotāynirujjhatīti    pe    ghānāy manāy dhammāynirujjhatīti yassakaṃ pi yassayatthakaṃ pi sadisaṃ citthāretabbaṃ i Yassa cakkhāy na nirujjhati tassa sotāy na nirujjhatīti Acakkhukānaṃ sasotakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ cakkhāy na nirujjhati no ca tesaṃ sotāy na nirujjhatisabbesaṃ uppajjantānaṃ acakkhukānaṃ asotakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ cakkhāy ca na nirujjhati sotāy ca na nirujjhati Yassa vā pana sotāy na nirujjhati tassa cakkhāy na nirujjhatīti Asotakānaṃ sacakkhukānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ sotāy na nirujjhati no ca tesaṃ cakkhāyna nirujjhati sabbesaṃ uppajjantānaṃ acakkhukānaṃ asotakānaṃ cavantānaṃ tesaṃ sotāy                      Āyatanayamakaṃca nirujjhati cakkhāy ca na nirujjhatiYassa cakkhāy na nirujjhati tassa ghānāy na nuppajjati no ca tesaṃ tattha maggas nuppajjittha suddhāvāsānaṃ dutiye citte pavattamāne anabhisametāvīnaṃ taṇhāya bhaṅgakkhaṇe taṇhāvippayuttacitte pavattamāne asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha samudayas Yassa dukkhas na nirujjhati tassa samudayas na nirujjhatīti Āmantā Yassa vā pana samudayas na nirujjhati                      Saccayamakaṃtassa dukkhas na nirujjhatīti Sabbesaṃ cavantānaṃ pavatte pucchā anulomaṃ pi paccaniyaṃ pi vibhattaṃ evaṃ Nirodhe pi vibhajitabbaṃ natthi nānākaraṇaṃ i Yassa dukkhas nirujjhissati tassa samudayasnirujjhissatīti Aggamaggasamaṅgīnaṃ arahantānaṃ yassa cittassa anantarā aggamaggaṃ paṭilabhissanti tassa cittassa uppādakkhaṇe  tesaṃ dukkhas nirujjhissati no ca tesaṃ samudayas nirujjhissati itaresaṃ dukkhas    samudayas ca nirujjhissati Y v p samudayas uppajjati tassa kāmarāgānusayo uppajjatīti Āmantā                      AnusayayamakaṃYassa kāmarāgānusayo uppajjati tassa mānānusayo uppajjatīti Āmantā Yassa vā pana mānānusayo uppajjatitassa kāmarāgānusayo uppajjatīti Anāgāmissa mānānusayo uppajjati no ca tassa kāmarāgānusayo uppajjatitiṇṇaṃ puggalānaṃ mānānusayo ca uppajjati kāmarāgānusayo ca uppajjati VitthāretabbaṃYassa kāmarāgānusayo nuppajjati tassa paṭighānusayo nuppajjatīti Āmantā Yassa vā pana paṭighānusayo nuppajjati tassa kāmarāgānusayo nuppajjatīti ĀmantāYassa kāmarāgānusayo nuppajjati tassa mānānusayo nuppajjatīti
